winners; Christie Jernsteadt and Jam Heinrich, Hood River,
runners up. Scores: 6-3, 3-6, 7-5.

Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 6:43 pm 6/6/2024.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place singles
or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of seven (7) points.
The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of eight (8) points. The singles and doubles team
champions will each earn a total of ten (10) points. If a player receives a bye in the first round of the main draw, four
(4) points are given only if the second-round match is won.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and one half
(.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will each receive one
(1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 32
2 = Second Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = First Consolation Round (no points)
C2 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2024 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 6:43 pm 6/6/2024.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place singles
or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of five (5) points. The
singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of six (6) points. The singles and doubles team champions
will each earn a total of eight (8) points.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (0.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and one half
(.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will each receive one
(1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2024 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 6:43 pm 6/6/2024.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place singles
or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of seven (7) points.
The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of eight (8) points. The singles and doubles team
champions will each earn a total of ten (10) points. If a player receives a bye in the first round of the main draw, four
(4) points are given only if the second-round match is won.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and one half
(.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will each receive one
(1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 32
2 = Second Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = First Consolation Round (no points)
C2 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2024 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 6:43 pm 6/6/2024.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place singles
or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of seven (7) points.
The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of eight (8) points. The singles and doubles team
champions will each earn a total of ten (10) points. If a player receives a bye in the first round of the main draw, four
(4) points are given only if the second-round match is won.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and one half
(.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will each receive one
(1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 32
2 = Second Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = First Consolation Round (no points)
C2 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2024 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 6:43 pm 6/6/2024.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place singles
or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of five (5) points. The
singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of six (6) points. The singles and doubles team champions
will each earn a total of eight (8) points.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (0.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and one half
(.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will each receive one
(1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2024 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 6:43 pm 6/6/2024.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place singles
or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of seven (7) points.
The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of eight (8) points. The singles and doubles team
champions will each earn a total of ten (10) points. If a player receives a bye in the first round of the main draw, four
(4) points are given only if the second-round match is won.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and one half
(.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will each receive one
(1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 32
2 = Second Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = First Consolation Round (no points)
C2 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2025 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 10:48 am 6/10/2025.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place
singles or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of
seven (7) points. The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of eight (8) points. The
singles and doubles team champions will each earn a total of ten (10) points. If a player receives a bye in the
first round of the main draw, four (4) points are given only if the second-round match is won.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and
one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will
each receive one (1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 32
2 = Second Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = First Consolation Round (no points)
C2 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2025 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 10:48 am 6/10/2025.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place
singles or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of five
(5) points. The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of six (6) points. The singles and
doubles team champions will each earn a total of eight (8) points.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (0.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and
one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will
each receive one (1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2025 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 10:48 am 6/10/2025.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place
singles or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of
seven (7) points. The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of eight (8) points. The
singles and doubles team champions will each earn a total of ten (10) points. If a player receives a bye in the
first round of the main draw, four (4) points are given only if the second-round match is won.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and
one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will
each receive one (1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 32
2 = Second Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = First Consolation Round (no points)
C2 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2025 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 10:48 am 6/10/2025.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place
singles or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of five
(5) points. The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of six (6) points. The singles and
doubles team champions will each earn a total of eight (8) points.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (0.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and
one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will
each receive one (1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match

2025 Tennis State Championship Team Scores
Team scores were last calculated 10:48 am 6/10/2025.
Team Scoring
Each singles player or doubles team receives two (2) points for each win in the main draw. The 3rd/4th place
singles or doubles team winner receives one (1) additional point for winning that match, earning a total of
seven (7) points. The singles and doubles team runners-up will each earn a total of eight (8) points. The
singles and doubles team champions will each earn a total of ten (10) points. If a player receives a bye in the
first round of the main draw, four (4) points are given only if the second-round match is won.
Each singles player or doubles team receives one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation semifinals and
one half (.5) point for reaching the consolation final. The singles and doubles team consolation winner will
each receive one (1) point for winning the consolation final, earning a total of two (2) points.
Scoring Legend [Round +Points]:
1 = First Round / Round of 32
2 = Second Round / Round of 16
QF = Quarterfinal Round
SF = Semifinal Round
F = Championship Final Match
S = 3rd/4th Place Match
C1 = First Consolation Round (no points)
C2 = Consolation Quarterfinal Round
SC = Consolation Semifinal Round
C = Consolation Final Match
